word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	不少人早上睡到七八点还觉得很困，觉得头上有东西裹着，让人打不起精神。或觉得身上有东西包着，让人懒得动弹，中医形容其为&ldquo;湿重如裹&rdquo;。这种被包裹着的感觉其实就是身体对湿气的感受，好像穿着一件洗过没干的衬衫似的那么别扭，由此可以判断体内有湿了。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; font-size: 16px; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	清晨方便后，可以观察一下大便是不是老是粘在马桶上，冲不净。如果大便不成形、便溏，提示体内有湿。如果大便成形，但大便完了之后总会有一些粘在马桶上，很难冲下去，这也是体内有湿的一种表现，因为湿气有黏腻的特点。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	在刷牙前不妨对着镜子看看自己的舌头。&ldquo;舌为心之苗，又为脾之外候&rdquo;，舌头可以敏感地反映出我们的身体状况。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; text-align: center; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	<img _src=\"http://01.imgmini.eastday.com/mobile/20180507/20180507205722_e0d96364bbc07b4fd6425dec2497b311_2.jpeg\" alt=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.66796875\" data-type=\"png\" src=\"http://01.imgmini.eastday.com/mobile/20180507/20180507205722_e0d96364bbc07b4fd6425dec2497b311_2.jpeg\" style=\"margin: 0px; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	健康的舌淡红而润泽，舌面有一层舌苔，薄白而清净、干湿适中、不滑不燥。如果舌头达不到这些指标，那说明身体机能已经出现问题了。如果舌苔白厚，看起来滑而湿润，则说明体内有寒；如果舌苔粗糙或很厚、发黄发腻，则说明体内有湿热；如果舌质赤红无苔，则说明体内已经热到一定的程度，伤阴了。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	玉米须，在中医药中叫做龙须，中医认为，玉米须性平，味甘、淡，归膀胱、肝、胆经。利水、消肿、泄热，可促进体内多余水分代谢，减少头发皮肤出油，消除小腹赘肉，对肾炎、肝炎、胆囊炎、胆结石等有效，尤其适合血糖高者。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; text-align: center; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	<img _src=\"http://www.zgys.net/uploads/allimg/180130/4-1P130191K9.jpg\" alt=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.66796875\" data-type=\"png\" src=\"http://www.zgys.net/uploads/allimg/180130/4-1P130191K9.jpg\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	蒲公英入肝胆经，又称&ldquo;尿床草&rdquo;，利尿效果俱佳，可以帮助身体排出更多的水分，并且蒲公英有&ldquo;天然抗生素&rdquo;之称，抗菌消炎，清热解毒，在增加排尿量的同时，还可以对尿路起到冲刷消炎的作用，对尿路感染也有好处，不过，服用蒲公英之前一定要做好辩证工作，同时还要科学服用，这对于身体才是最好的选择，二十八珍膏把蒲公英与其他二十余种中药材科学配比，古方熬制，祛湿效果既快又好，有效率高达九五成以上，已经传承了百余年，早就被列为非物质文化遗产，搭配开水食用方便，在网上即可找到，蒲公英清热解，清肝火胃火，对于去除口臭有帮助。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	<span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; line-height: inherit;\">避免潮湿环境。</span><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; line-height: inherit;\">在低温时，潮湿加强了空气对热的传导作用，使体热大量散失，故在低温潮湿的情况下，机体更易受寒冷的损害，易发生风湿病和支气管炎。</span></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; text-align: center; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	<span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; line-height: inherit;\"><img _src=\"http://7xkq88.com1.z0.glb.clouddn.com/1835669-temp-201806-01-1527825873505.jpg\" alt=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.66796875\" data-type=\"png\" src=\"http://7xkq88.com1.z0.glb.clouddn.com/1835669-temp-201806-01-1527825873505.jpg\" style=\"margin: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	<span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; line-height: inherit;\">此外，潮湿环境对结核病、肾脏病、风湿性关节炎、慢性腰腿痛等病患者都有不良的影响。倘若在热环境中，相对湿度又太大时，有碍于机体蒸发散热。</span><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; line-height: inherit;\">日常生活注意减少暴露在潮湿环境中，还应注意不要穿潮湿未干的衣服，不要直接睡地板。</span></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	<span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; line-height: inherit;\">饮食清淡适量。肠胃系统攸关营养及水分代谢，最好的方式就是适量、均衡饮食。少食甜腻食物，避开生冷食物，少饮酒。</span><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; line-height: inherit;\">清淡的饮食可以有效的减少身体的负担，就像一个人没负担的走路一样，所以很多人都追求清淡的饮食习惯。预防疾病，清淡的饮食对那些有高血压，糖尿病，心脏病的中老年人来说是绝对必须的，坚持清淡的饮食是很好的预防疾病的方法。</span></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; text-align: center; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	<img _src=\"http://img.99.com.cn/uploads/170522/404_140628_1.jpg\" alt=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.66796875\" data-type=\"png\" src=\"http://img.99.com.cn/uploads/170522/404_140628_1.jpg\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	每天坚持适量的运动。一方面由于现在工作繁忙，很多人都处于亚健康的状态，缺乏运动，容易招惹湿气的侵袭。另一方面，由于夏季开空调，长时间处于寒凉的状态，导致身体很多水分来不及排出体外，造成湿气过重。适量的运动，排汗，有助于湿气排出体外，也是最有效的方式。运动可以纾解压力、活络身体器官运作，加速湿气排出体外。可以试试跑步、健走、游泳、瑜珈、太极等运动，有助活化气血循环，增加水分代谢。运动出汗是很好的去湿气的方法。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	湿气还会极大的影响一个人的容貌，表现在皮肤上会出现长斑长痘，暗黄无光；表现在体型上就是水肿肥胖，大腹便便。表现在精神气色上就会出现无精打采，困乏无力。 湿气还会引起头脸油腻，皮肤松驰、色斑、痘痘、湿疹等诸多皮肤问题，体内的湿气除掉后能一起修复这些因湿气而引起的皮肤问题。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	中医认为，环境气候会对人的身体产生重要的影响，当环境潮湿阴凉时，人体很容易遭受湿气侵犯。由于&ldquo;湿&rdquo;是引发及恶化疾病的关键，因此人体祛湿尤为重要。那么，人体有湿气该怎么祛湿呢?</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	作用：冬瓜鲫鱼汤有利小便、消水肿、清热毒、止烦渴的作用，在闷热的夏季经常服食祛暑湿的效果还不错。鲫鱼要先经油煎，炖出来的汤才会浓白醇香，鱼肉的营养成分经油溶解后更易于人体吸收。煎鱼的时候锅要烧热，油也要烧热，放鱼的时候要缓而准，放下去之后先不要急着动它，估计一面煎的差不多了，晃一下锅，鱼能离锅滑动的时候，用锅铲伸到鱼身下方中间的位置，快速的翻身再煎另一面。鲫鱼若经煎炸则食疗功效会打些折扣。鲫鱼子中胆固醇含量较高，故中老年人和高血脂、高胆固醇者应尽量少食。鲫鱼细刺较多，老年人、儿童食用时需缓慢进食，并耐心剔除鱼刺。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	2、红枣薏米汁</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	作用：很多人可能都觉得湿气重的不适合再吃红枣了，其实不然，红枣能够健脾益气，促进脾胃代谢水湿；而薏米性凉，不仅可以解暑，还是很好的利湿材料，二者结合非常适合夏季湿气重的人饮用，但是要注意把握比例。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; text-align: center; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	<img _src=\"http://7xkq88.com1.z0.glb.clouddn.com/1835669-temp-201806-01-1527838175799.jpg\" alt=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.66796875\" data-type=\"png\" src=\"http://7xkq88.com1.z0.glb.clouddn.com/1835669-temp-201806-01-1527838175799.jpg\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	3、绿豆薏米粥</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	作用：绿豆可清热解毒，薏米能够健脾祛湿，经常食用绿豆薏米粥是非常不错的选择。绿豆性寒凉，素体阳虚、脾胃虚寒、泄泻者慎食，古方二十八珍膏祛湿很温和，富含薏米、红豆、山药、葛根、蒲公英等多种有效成分，健脾利胃，清热排毒，给身体虚弱，脾胃不好的人带来了福音，搭配开水服用即可，小孩子也可以食用，因为它是带着甜味的，另外临床数据都表明了其有效率高达九五成以上，已经被列为非物质文化遗产，网上就可以找得到，注意在服温补药时不宜食用绿豆，以免降低药效。绿豆有解毒作用，如果服用的药物中含有有机磷、钙、钾等成分，绿豆会与这些成分结合成沉淀物，从而分解药效，影响效果。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	生活习惯要良好：</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	1、注重热养生</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	经常汗蒸是辅助湿气排出的有效方法，能使得身体的温度不断升高，能促进肌肤毛孔的打开，从而增强身体的新陈代谢机制。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; text-align: center; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	<img _src=\"http://pic.eastlady.cn/jzpt/201704/149058347789239.jpg\" alt=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.66796875\" data-type=\"png\" src=\"http://pic.eastlady.cn/jzpt/201704/149058347789239.jpg\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	汗蒸过后的身体一定还要注意保暖，居室要常通风，多抽湿。祛外湿，不要久居潮湿之地，尽量不要到外面潮湿的地方劳作。湿气大、阴雨天时不要常开窗，但最好仍保持通风。注意室内的抽风和抽湿。即使衣服难干也不要勉强穿不干的衣服。更重要的是，如果家里有小孩，记得保持玩具的清洁，不给病菌入侵的机会。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	另外，如果体内的湿气实在太重，选择拔火罐也是不错的选择。但是无论是汗蒸和拔火罐，一定要讲究方法，也勿要过于频繁。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	2、运动得坚持</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; text-align: center; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	<img _src=\"http://img18.3lian.com/d/file/201711/04/a00eb5d2f6392c2851f7dfc258988497.png\" alt=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.66796875\" data-type=\"png\" src=\"http://img18.3lian.com/d/file/201711/04/a00eb5d2f6392c2851f7dfc258988497.png\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	日常运动少了，身体自然也会很少流汗，于是各种湿寒暑热之气便通通&ldquo;隐藏&rdquo;在体内，而如果每天都能适量的运动一会，这便能有效的促进全身的血液循环，而在血液运行的过程中，也能将湿气慢慢&ldquo;携&rdquo;出体外，帮你解除后患。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	因此，千万别总说没时间运动，人只要一懒，体质就会变差哦!况且是本身湿气就重的人，所以，赶紧迈开腿运动吧!</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	&nbsp;</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	<span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; line-height: inherit;\">淡竹叶薏仁茶出自《本草纲目》。具体做法是将薏米仁炒到微黄，将薏米仁、槐米、赤小豆各5克用冷水浸泡半天，洗净后加水煮一小时，再加入1克淡竹叶、马齿苋、芡实、绿茶等食材，转文火煮半小时，待凉饮用。不想动手做的也可以喝袋泡茶。</span></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	<span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 宋体; line-height: inherit;\">祛湿原理分析：淡竹叶始载于《本草纲目》。淡竹叶的利尿作用较好，以渗湿泄热见长。能清心、利尿、祛烦躁，解渴消暑，解毒利尿。赤小豆薏米能健脾祛湿、固肾止泻，槐米泄肺逆，泻心火，清肝火，坚肾水。绿茶不发酵，有祛湿的效果，马齿苋清热解毒，利水去湿，散血消肿之效。</span></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; text-align: center; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	<span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	吃肉吃得太多，吃的食物里有污染，运动量少，身体阴盛阳虚，湿邪内郁，所以大便无法正常。为什么成型的大便很少呢？中医里讲，脾虚则便溏，中国人本应以五谷杂粮为食，以肉食为主了，很多人一天不吃肉就觉得很亏，长期这样，伤害的是脾胃，脾是运化水湿的，脾受到伤害，水湿不能完全运化，就在身体内堆积。所以，大便不成形意味着脾虚，也意味着体内有湿气。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	体内湿气重的表现</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	吃肉吃得太多，吃的食物里有污染，运动量少，身体阴盛阳虚，湿邪内郁，所以大便无法正常。为什么成型的大便很少呢？中医里讲，脾虚则便溏，中国人本应以五谷杂粮为食，以肉食为主了，很多人一天不吃肉就觉得很亏，长期这样，伤害的是脾胃，脾是运化水湿的，脾受到伤害，水湿不能完全运化，就在身体内堆积。所以，大便不成形意味着脾虚，也意味着体内有湿气。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	体内湿气重的人大多数都是饮食油腻、缺乏运动的人,而同时他们又常常会因为湿气重而感觉身体沉重四肢无力,这样形成了一种恶性循环,越是不爱运动,体内淤积的湿气就越多,久而久之,必然就会导致湿气攻入脾脏,引发一系列的重症。可通过日常饮食去除体内湿气，但是一定要明确该吃什么，不该吃什么，否则湿气加重会得不偿失。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	1、湿气重的人不要吃太凉的事物。总体来说,寒凉、粘腻、不好消化的都要小心些,但具体食物要看做法和季节,比方植物中的瓜类,夏季适当吃无妨,入秋后其寒凉性比较突出;又比如鸡平和微温(而鸭相对来说认为偏阴偏湿),不过做得油腻的话,湿气重的吃了鸡一样有一定的反应。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	2、诸如此类例子很多很多,虽然食物的确有种种偏性,但是机械地说什么能吃什么不能吃并不妥,食物最好保持一定多样性,不要过于偏食,只要注意其性质有所侧重就行。所以正确的办法是多去理解中医说的&ldquo;湿&rdquo;是怎么一个原理(从中医原理的角度),然后再去研究你常吃得到的食物会是怎么回事,这样更有利于养生健康。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: center;\">\r\n	<img _src=\"http://7xkq88.com1.z0.glb.clouddn.com/1835669-temp-201806-02-1527921550835.jpg\" alt=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.66796875\" data-type=\"png\" src=\"http://7xkq88.com1.z0.glb.clouddn.com/1835669-temp-201806-02-1527921550835.jpg\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	1、蒜是很好的祛湿食材。可以多吃蒜苗,夏天做菜的时候可以多加蒜蓉调味,做瘦肉粥或是肉骨粥等荤粥品的时候可以加点蒜瓣,炖汤则可以加点大蒜姜也是祛湿良品,平常做菜肴可以适当加些姜蓉姜片调味,也可以做子姜为主食材的菜肴(姜爆鸭、子姜炒肉片、子姜炖牛肉等),常水中作业的人群则建议常喝甜酒姜汤。对于那些不喜欢葱姜蒜的人群来说，古方二.十.八.珍.膏是不二之选，每天搭配开水食用一包简直是方便快捷，重点是祛湿效果既快又好，给生活忙碌的人带来了福音，有效率高达九五成以上，不必担心有任何副作用，被誉为非遗，网上就可以找到，紫姜的祛湿效果最好,建议食用紫姜。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	2、紫苏是调味香料,也是祛湿良品。做鱼类、贝壳类、海鲜、田螺等水产菜肴的时候,可以多加点鲜紫苏叶或是紫苏粉,不但能去腥,还能祛湿气。此外,也可以用紫苏炖肉来祛湿,建议紫苏炖羊肉或是紫苏炖牛肉。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	<img _src=\"http://stc.zjol.com.cn/g1/M000897CggSDlbFe1qAOm8UAAORjjrHGaY313.jpg?width=720&amp;height=540\" alt=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.66796875\" data-type=\"png\" src=\"http://stc.zjol.com.cn/g1/M000897CggSDlbFe1qAOm8UAAORjjrHGaY313.jpg?width=720&amp;height=540\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	3、辣椒也是祛湿良品。比较辣的辣椒只能用来做菜肴调味,肯定不能大量吃的。如果吃不了辣,就多吃甜椒、菜椒等不辣或微辣的辣椒品种。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	4、红豆(赤小豆)中药材名，为豆科植物红豆树的种子，秋末冬初采种子，备用。它主要可以理气，通经，治疝气，腹痛，血滞经闭，也是祛湿良品，但是体虚多汗、咳嗽咯血及孕妇忌服。可以用红豆做杂粮粥品,也可以用红豆炖骨头汤,推荐蒜瓣红豆筒骨粥。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: center;\">\r\n	<img _src=\"http://simg.dahe.cn/2016/6/1/b2aa10bae71c7c01.jpg\" alt=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.66796875\" data-type=\"png\" src=\"http://simg.dahe.cn/2016/6/1/b2aa10bae71c7c01.jpg\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	5、酒是祛湿良品,有节制适量喝酒对去湿气很有效。如果不能喝酒,则可以用酒做姜汤(往姜汤里加点酒),如果能耐住那个酒味,就用白酒;如果完全喝不惯酒,就加甜酒或是黄酒。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	湿气重还要做什么？</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	1、勤运动</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	湿气重的人可以通过运动来缓解压力，促进身体新陈代谢，排出湿气。跑步、游泳、瑜伽、太极等都是很好的选择，加速血液循环。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	2、多做深呼吸</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	深呼吸有利于调整我们的肺功能，也会让我们的湿气消失。因为湿气会随着呼吸呼出，并且保持通畅。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: center;\">\r\n	<img _src=\"http://7xkq88.com1.z0.glb.clouddn.com/1835669-temp-201806-02-1527921644155.jpg\" alt=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.66796875\" data-type=\"png\" src=\"http://7xkq88.com1.z0.glb.clouddn.com/1835669-temp-201806-02-1527921644155.jpg\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	3、避开环境的湿气</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	不要直接睡地板。地板湿气重，容易入侵体内，造成四肢酸痛；潮湿下雨天减少外出；不要穿潮湿未干的衣服，不要盖潮湿的被子，洗完澡后要充分擦干身体，吹干头发；房间内的湿气如果很重，建议多开窗透气。如果外界湿气也很重，还可以打开风扇、空调，借助这些电器保持空气的对流。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	体内湿气重的人大多数都是饮食油腻、缺乏运动的人,而同时他们又常常会因为湿气重而感觉身体沉重四肢无力,这样形成了一种恶性循环,越是不爱运动,体内淤积的湿气就越多,久而久之,必然就会导致湿气攻入脾脏,引发一系列的重症。</h2>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	夏天已经到了，酷热的高温让人的食欲也大减，每天的食谱，该吃点什么饭呢？而且又能保持身体健康呢？是好多人纠结的问题，下面介绍几种菜可通过日常饮食帮助大家去除体内湿气,那么有哪些食物具有祛湿功能呢?</h2>\r\n<h2 style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-weight: 400; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	1、绿豆芽</h2>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	绿豆芽的营养价值也毫不逊色,它不仅含有蛋白质、胡萝卜素、钙、磷、铁等多种矿物质,而且还含有丰富的维生素,特别是维生素C的含量尤其丰富。虽然绿豆芽、黄豆芽均性寒味甘,但作用不同。绿豆芽具有清热解毒、利尿除湿的作用。适用于饮酒过度、湿热郁滞、口干口渴、小便赤热、便秘、目赤肿痛等患者食用。黄豆芽具有清热解毒、降血压、美肌肤的作用。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	黄花菜是一种多年生草本植物的花蕾,味鲜质嫩,营养丰富,含有丰富的花粉、糖、蛋白质、维生素C、钙、脂肪、胡萝卜素、氨基酸等人体所必须的养分,其所含的胡萝卜素甚至超过西红柿的几倍。有清热、利湿、利尿、健胃消食、明目、安神、止血、通乳、消肿等功能。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	3、大头菜</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	大头菜,又称芜菁、芥辣、芥菜疙瘩,是芥菜的一个变种,为根用芥菜。它质地紧密,水份少,纤维多,有强烈的芥辣味并稍带苦味。芥菜类蔬菜有清热解毒、抗菌消肿的作用,能抗感染和预防疾病的发生,抑制细菌毒素的毒性,促进伤口愈合。大头菜性平,味苦、辛、甘,入胃、肝、肾经,能利尿除湿,促进机体水、电解质平衡,具有开胃下气、祛湿解毒的作用。适于治疗食积不化、消渴、热毒风肿等病症。大头菜风味佳,可以代粮,也可做菜用,或盐渍加工。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	马齿苋属一年生肉质草本植物。因其营养丰富,食疗作用显着,食之益人,可延年益寿,故又美其名日:&ldquo;长命菜&rdquo;。 中医认为马齿苋有清热解毒祛湿、凉血止痢消肿的作用。治疗湿热痢疾、疮疡肿毒、湿疹皮炎、蛇虫伤、崩漏、产后出血、妇女赤白带下、痔疮出血、乳疮、百日咳等症。对于预防肠道传染病效果尤其好,所以保健要多吃马齿苋，马齿苋也是古方二十八珍膏中的一种有效成分，此外该方还有其它二十多种优质中药材，强强联合，旨在健脾利胃，清热祛湿，有效率高达九五成以上，很早就被誉为非物质文化遗产，网上就能找到，是不可多得的良品。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: center;\">\r\n	<img _src=\"http://7xkq88.com1.z0.glb.clouddn.com/1835669-temp-201806-02-1527925934766.jpg\" alt=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.66796875\" data-type=\"png\" src=\"http://7xkq88.com1.z0.glb.clouddn.com/1835669-temp-201806-02-1527925934766.jpg\" style=\"margin: 0px; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	5、苦瓜</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	苦瓜气味苦、无毒、性寒,入心、肝、脾、肺经,具有清热祛暑、明目解毒、降压降糖、利尿凉血、解劳清心、益气之功能。由于苦瓜内含奎宁,具有清热解毒、祛湿止痒之功。可用于治疗热毒、疖疮、痱子、湿疹等病症。此外,苦瓜的维生素C含量很高,具有预防坏血病、保护细胞膜、防止动脉粥样硬化、提高机体应激能力、保护心脏等作用,但是也不要多吃。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: center;\">\r\n	<img _src=\"http://www.1ms.cn/uploads/allimg/170613/143GE0C_0.jpg\" alt=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.66796875\" data-type=\"png\" src=\"http://www.1ms.cn/uploads/allimg/170613/143GE0C_0.jpg\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	既然吃饭吃的健康了，那么适量的运动也是每天必备的功课，运动可以纾解压力、活络身体器官运作，加速湿气排出体外。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	现代人动脑多、体力消耗少，加上长期待在密闭空调内，很少流汗，身体调控湿度的能力变差。试试看跑步、健走、游泳、瑜珈、太极等任何「有点喘、会流汗」的运动，有助活化气血循环，增加水分代谢。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: center;\">\r\n	<img _src=\"http://7xkq88.com1.z0.glb.clouddn.com/1835669-temp-201806-02-1527925996998.jpg\" alt=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.66796875\" data-type=\"png\" src=\"http://7xkq88.com1.z0.glb.clouddn.com/1835669-temp-201806-02-1527925996998.jpg\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	​</p>\r\n','','','182.124.16.76');
INSERT INTO `dede_addonarticle` VALUES('32','4','<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	湿气一般是由外湿气入侵体内产生内湿气，如经常淋雨、穿湿衣服、太冷衣服穿的少等等；同时饮食不当也可能产生内湿气，比如夏天吃冰棍伤了脾脏，影响体内水分的排出，多余的水分停滞在体内就形成了湿气。体内湿气过重，会让人觉得困倦、身体四支沉重、没有食欲、手脚冰冷、皮肤起疹、脸上黏腻不舒服，甚至出现肠胃炎现象，口腔症状比较明显，舌苔白厚。要去除体内的湿气，首先要从改善日常生活习惯做起。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; text-align: center; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	<img _src=\"http://pic.qbaobei.com/Uploads/Editor/2016-07-01/5775d56707953.jpg\" alt=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.66796875\" data-type=\"png\" src=\"http://pic.qbaobei.com/Uploads/Editor/2016-07-01/5775d56707953.jpg\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	体内湿气重应该如何调理？</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	1、采取运动出汗方式祛湿调理</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	慢跑或者散步,让身体适当流汗,能去除身体的晦气和湿气。让机能健康起来,自然就平衡了,运动出汗是很好的去湿气方式。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	2、用祛湿的汤或粥去湿气来调理</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	对于湿热体质人群来说,去湿气的粥和汤水是很好的选择。比如用茯苓、薏米、红豆、绿豆等煮成的粥,健脾祛湿还养胃。以及,用冬瓜、排骨、莲子等煮成汤,可以清热利湿。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; text-align: center; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	<img _src=\"http://7xkq88.com1.z0.glb.clouddn.com/1835669-temp-201806-03-1527986689244.jpg\" alt=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.66796875\" data-type=\"png\" src=\"http://7xkq88.com1.z0.glb.clouddn.com/1835669-temp-201806-03-1527986689244.jpg\" style=\"margin: 0px; font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	需要注意:去湿气的红豆薏米粥忌加大米,因为大米长在水里,含有湿气,这样就破坏了红豆薏米粥的效果了。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	茯苓粥&mdash;&mdash;健脾祛湿</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	取粳米100克,淘净;粳米100克、茯苓粉20克一起放入锅中,加入适量水,调至武火将水烧沸,水开后转用文火熬至糜烂,然后加入盐、生姜粒若干,搅匀即成。每天早晚各服用一次,根据口味可加入红糖。长期食用可起到利水渗温、健脾祛湿,对于慢性肝炎也有一定的效果。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; text-align: center; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	<img _src=\"http://s13.sinaimg.cn/mw690/001cnLgSty71zRfxo6M8c&amp;690\" alt=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.66796875\" data-type=\"png\" src=\"http://s13.sinaimg.cn/mw690/001cnLgSty71zRfxo6M8c&amp;690\" style=\"margin: 0px; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	冬瓜粥&mdash;&mdash;利尿祛湿</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	冬瓜100克,粳米100克。冬瓜洗净,带皮切成小块,和粳米一起放入沙锅加水,文火熬煮至瓜烂米熟成粥即成。冬瓜含有丰富的维生素和人体必需的微量元素,并能利尿祛湿,同时也是消暑佳品。此粥根据口味可做成甜或咸的,最佳食用时间是每天上午和下午的餐饮时间。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	<img _src=\"http://i5.xiachufang.com/image/620/4a008838d34b11e3865be0db5512b208.jpg\" alt=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.66796875\" data-type=\"png\" src=\"http://i5.xiachufang.com/image/620/4a008838d34b11e3865be0db5512b208.jpg\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	参芪粥&mdash;&mdash;祛湿</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	需要准备的材料是,15g的黄芪和党参,60g的炒薏米,15g炒扁豆,2个红枣,还有100g大米。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	先将薏米、扁豆炒至微黄,红枣去核,用清水洗净黄芪、党参并放入砂锅内,加水煎汁。药汁熬好后,去除药渣,将炒薏米、炒扁豆、红枣肉、大米一同放进药汁中煮沸,后用文火煮成粥。但是现在的生活节奏普遍加快，很多人并没有太多的时间去煲粥，建议选择二十八珍膏，除了上述的那些优质中药材之外，还有二十多种，该方采用黄金比例搭配，健脾利胃，缓解身体上的各种不适，坚持服用，湿气可尽数除去，有效率高达九五成以上，不会产生任何副作用，被誉为非遗，网上就能找到。黄芪、党参具有健脾益气的作用,薏米、扁豆能够祛湿,做成能够养胃的粥,可补中益气,健脾祛湿,缓解湿盛带来的身体不适。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	3、常吃发酵食物,帮助肠道代谢通畅</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; text-align: center; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	<img _src=\"http://7xkq88.com1.z0.glb.clouddn.com/1835669-temp-201806-03-1527986784503.jpg\" alt=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.66796875\" data-type=\"png\" src=\"http://7xkq88.com1.z0.glb.clouddn.com/1835669-temp-201806-03-1527986784503.jpg\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	日常生活中经常食用的发面食物、酱油、食醋、豆豉、腐乳、黄酒、啤酒等等都是发酵食物,中医认为都是养脾胃的。西方营养学家也证实,发酵食物是人类健康饮食结构的有益补充,能帮助人们的肠道代谢更顺畅。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	下面的几方面也应该尽力做到，才能更好地帮助排除体内的湿气。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	1、勤运动</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	湿气重的人可以通过运动来缓解压力，促进身体新陈代谢，排出湿气。跑步、游泳、瑜伽、太极等都是很好的选择，加速血液循环。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	不要直接睡地板。地板湿气重，容易入侵体内，造成四肢酸痛；潮湿下雨天减少外出；不要穿潮湿未干的衣服，不要盖潮湿的被子，洗完澡后要充分擦干身体，吹干头发；房间内的湿气如果很重，建议多开窗透气。如果外界湿气也很重，还可以打开风扇、空调，借助这些电器保持空气的对流。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; word-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 微软雅黑;\">湿气入皮下,会影响皮肤细胞的新陈代谢,降低脂肪燃烧效率,从而导致肥胖。过多的湿气滞留在体内,加重脾运化水湿的负担,就像马车超载一样,有时甚至会影响肾的利尿功能,严重的可继发全身浮肿。</span></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; text-align: center; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	<span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 微软雅黑;\"><img _src=\"http://img1.gtimg.com/hn/pics/hv1/82/110/2193/142627957.jpg\" alt=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.66796875\" data-type=\"png\" src=\"http://img1.gtimg.com/hn/pics/hv1/82/110/2193/142627957.jpg\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></span></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	<span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 微软雅黑;\">2、伤害关节</span></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	<span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 微软雅黑;\">湿气进入关节,与&ldquo;寒&rdquo;相遇,会形成寒湿,是引发炎症,导致关节疼痛的重要原因。</span></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	<span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 微软雅黑;\">3、影响排泄</span></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	<span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 微软雅黑;\">湿气过重,会造成&ldquo;湿气黏肠&rdquo;,大便次数增多,且有拉不干净的感觉。中医说,&ldquo;湿气如裹&rdquo;,湿气重会影响细胞间的通透性,就像一床湿棉被盖在人的身上一样,会让你常常有头沉、无精打采的感觉。</span></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	<span style=\"margin: 0px; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	<span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: 微软雅黑;\">薏仁可促进体内血液循环、水分代谢,发挥利尿消肿的效果,有助于改善水肿型肥胖。薏仁水是不错的排毒方法,直接将薏仁用开水煮烂后,适个人口味添加少许的糖,是肌肤美白的天然保养品。</span></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	湿气，是中医所说风、寒、暑、湿、燥、火六种病邪之一。如果体内湿气重，就会导致水湿内阻，常常引起全身的不适，其原因是湿气会侵入五脏六腑：湿在脾，则脾虚，湿在胃，则胃弱，湿在肾，则肾虚，湿在肺，则肺弱。五脏六腑不调和，湿气根本不可能完全祛除。湿气会在外导致很多表症，如皮肤油腻，口干口苦，嗓子干痒，长痘，湿疹，腰酸背痛等等。那么，人为什么有湿气？湿气怎么治？</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	人体内存有湿气，究其原因，不外乎外因与内因所致。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	外因：外在的环境，也就是湿邪进入到了身体。比如长期呆在湿气重的地方，比如淋了雨还不及时擦干，比如晚上洗头没吹干就睡觉，让外界的湿气进入到体内。湿气进入身体后常常奔着脾胃去，导致脾的运化能力下降，而这又会容易导致体内生湿。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: center;\">\r\n	<img _src=\"http://5b0988e595225.cdn.sohucs.com/images/20170827/d093c00c9d1e44caa8f3d32a56c874e9.jpeg\" alt=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.66796875\" data-type=\"png\" src=\"http://5b0988e595225.cdn.sohucs.com/images/20170827/d093c00c9d1e44caa8f3d32a56c874e9.jpeg\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	内因： 脾胃虚弱，饮食不当、习惯差，导致脾运化能力下降而生湿。脾主运化，吃进来的食物通过它来运化出精微物质，剩下的糟粕排出体外。当脾胃虚弱者，便会导致脾虚、运化能力下降的时候，精微物质就没法完全提炼出来。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	对付湿气，应注意以下几点：</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	1，饮食清淡适量。肠胃系统攸关营养及水分代谢，最好的方式就是适量、均衡饮食。少食甜腻食物，避开生冷食物，少饮酒。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: center;\">\r\n	<img _src=\"http://img.pcauto.com.cn/images/upload/upc/tx/auto5/1606/16/c0/22900054_1466039899181.jpg\" alt=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.66796875\" data-type=\"png\" src=\"http://img.pcauto.com.cn/images/upload/upc/tx/auto5/1606/16/c0/22900054_1466039899181.jpg\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	三款祛湿汤：</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	（1）健脾祛湿汤</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	脾虚湿困时，应健脾祛湿，把多余的水分排出体外（利尿）或者减少，清除引起身体免疫反应的物质，而温补脾胃是解除湿困的最好途径。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	淮山(干品)10克,土溪黄草10克,茯苓10克,猪胰(猪横月利)300克,清水适量。淮山、溪黄草、土茯苓、猪横月利洗净一同放进砂煲中,加适量清水煲开,然后转小火煲1小时即可饮用。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: center;\">\r\n	<img _src=\"http://uploads.oh100.com/allimg/1707/123-1FH5152641.jpg\" alt=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.66796875\" data-type=\"png\" src=\"http://uploads.oh100.com/allimg/1707/123-1FH5152641.jpg\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	（2）清热去湿汤</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	土伏苓250克,赤小豆50克,粉葛250克,扁豆50克,陈皮半个,水8碗。土伏苓去皮切段,将粉葛去皮切块,将材料放入煲内,水滚转慢火煲3小时即可。对于没有时间煲汤或者觉得麻烦的人群，建议尝试二十八珍膏，古方配置，内含二十多种祛湿成分，经过数道工序慢火熬制，小巧一包搭配开水冲服，带来了很大的方便，重点是能达到健脾利胃、清热解毒、快速根除湿气的效果，经过测试有效率高达九五成以上，被誉为非物质文化遗产，现在网上就能找到，想要清热平时就不要接触易上火的东西。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	（3）扁豆瘦肉汤</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	扁豆味甘，性微温，有健脾化湿，利尿消肿，清肝明目等作用。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: center;\">\r\n	<img _src=\"http://7xkq88.com1.z0.glb.clouddn.com/1835669-temp-201806-03-1527996777101.jpg\" alt=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.66796875\" data-type=\"png\" src=\"http://7xkq88.com1.z0.glb.clouddn.com/1835669-temp-201806-03-1527996777101.jpg\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	扁豆100克,陈皮1/4个、猪瘦肉400克,食盐、生姜适量。把猪肉切块洗净,陈皮去瓢,生姜切片;把1中的食材一同放进煲内,加入清水,先用大火煲沸后,改为小火煲1-1.5小时,加入适量食盐便可。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	2，避免潮湿环境。日常生活注意减少暴露在潮湿环境中，还应注意不要穿潮湿未干的衣服，不要直接睡地板。在低温时，潮湿加强了空气对热的传导作用，使体热大量散失，故在低温潮湿的情况下，机体更易受寒冷的损害，易发生风湿病和支气管炎。此外，潮湿环境对结核病、肾脏病、风湿性关节炎、慢性腰腿痛等病患者都有不良的影响。倘若在热环境中，相对湿度又太大时，有碍于机体蒸发散热。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: center;\">\r\n	<img _src=\"http://7xkq88.com1.z0.glb.clouddn.com/1835669-temp-201806-03-1527996867383.jpg\" alt=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.66796875\" data-type=\"png\" src=\"http://7xkq88.com1.z0.glb.clouddn.com/1835669-temp-201806-03-1527996867383.jpg\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	3，每天坚持适量的运动。运动可以纾解压力、活络身体器官运作，加速湿气排出体外。可以试试跑步、健走、游泳、瑜珈、太极等运动，有助活化气血循环，增加水分代谢。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	现代人是生活在一个冬有暖气夏有空调的环境中，对四季的感觉越来越不分明。夏天该出汗的时候因为用空调导致汗液挥发不出来淤积体内；冬天烧暖气，穿件单衣还冒汗，阳气外越，藏不住精气。（冬不藏精，春必病温）人体在这种环境的状态下最容易生病，皮肤开合的功能下降，抵御病邪的能力越来越差了，极容易导致体内湿邪堆积，造成阳气虚衰。湿邪对人体的伤害，比寒邪还要大。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	现在人，吃肉吃得太多，吃的食物里有污染，运动量少，身体阴盛阳虚，湿邪内郁，所以大便无法正常。为什么成型的大便很少呢？中医里讲，脾虚则便溏，中国人本应以五谷杂粮为食，现在以肉食为主了，很多人一天不吃肉就觉得很亏，长期这样，伤害的是脾胃脾是运化水湿的，脾受到伤害，水湿不能完全运化，就在身体内堆积。所以，大便不成形意味着脾虚，也意味着体内有湿气。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	湿气对于人体的危害可是很大的，那么该怎么祛除体内的湿气呢？夏天已经来了，好多水果都上市了，其实荔枝也是一种祛湿的好物呢，不妨听听下面的介绍吧。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	荔枝是一种很有营养价值的水果，虽然有些人不喜欢吃，说吃荔枝就有一种烂了的味道，但是夏季是荔枝火爆的季节，有很多人都会买一些荔枝来吃。那么，湿气重的人适合吃荔枝吗，有什么方法可以调理身体里的湿气呢？</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	荔枝种含有丰富的糖分，有补充能量，增强营养的作用；有研究证明，荔枝对大脑组织有补养作用，能有效改善失眠、健忘、神疲等症；荔枝种富含维生素C和蛋白质，有增强机体免疫功能，提高抗病能力的作用。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	1、消肿解毒，止血止痛。荔枝辛温，入肝、肾经，有理气止痛作用，可用于气滞血瘀所致的经前腹痛或者产后腹痛。还可用于外科疾病，如肿瘤、瘰疬、疔疮恶肿、外伤出血等病。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	2、促进血液循环。荔枝中含有丰富的维生素，可促进微细血管的血液循环，防止雀斑的发生，令皮肤更加光滑。其中富含维生素C，有助于增强集体的免疫力，提高抗病能力。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	4、补肝益脾、生津止渴等作用。《本草纲目》中有记载，荔枝有补脾益肝、生津止呃、消肿痛、镇咳养心等功能。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	体内湿气重的人大多数都是饮食油腻、缺乏运动的人。这些人常常会感觉身体沉重、四肢无力而不愿活动，但越是不爱运动，体内淤积的湿气就越多，久而久之，必然就会导致湿气攻入脾脏，引发一系列的病症。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;
