clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	①、阴陵泉穴</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	采用正坐或仰卧姿势，阴陵泉穴位于小腿内侧，在胫骨内侧髁后下方凹陷处，处于胫骨后缘和腓肠肌之间，比目鱼肌起点上。作用：体内有湿就容易感受外湿，别让体内湿邪太大，除了外散还要内化一部分。在阴陵泉穴的位置刮痧，可以起到内化湿邪的作用，还可清利湿热、健脾理气、益肾调经、通经活络，辅助缓解腹胀、泄泻、水肿、膝痛等。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; text-align: center; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	<img _src=\"http://img.cnys.com/upload/picture/2017/08-29/rKcabd.jpg\" alt=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.66796875\" data-type=\"png\" src=\"http://img.cnys.com/upload/picture/2017/08-29/rKcabd.jpg\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	<span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; line-height: inherit;\">②、血海穴</span></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	屈膝，在大腿内侧，髌底内侧端上两寸，股四头肌内侧头的隆起处。坐在椅子上将腿绷直后，会在膝盖内侧看到一个凹陷的地方，凹陷上方隆起的肌肉顶端就是血海穴。作用：可辅助缓解月经不调、闭经、气逆腹胀、湿疹、皮肤瘙痒、贫血等状况。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; text-align: center; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	<img _src=\"http://www.sztiantianai.com/uploads/allimg/170726/1-1FH61525162Y.jpg\" alt=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.66796875\" data-type=\"png\" src=\"http://www.sztiantianai.com/uploads/allimg/170726/1-1FH61525162Y.jpg\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	③、丰隆穴</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	在小腿前外侧，外踝尖上8寸，距胫骨前缘二横指(拇指)。作用：中医认为湿必生痰，此穴位可以化痰湿、清神志，尤其适合初秋里湿邪较盛的人群，可辅助缓解痰湿诱发的胸腹痛、呕吐、便秘、眩晕、烦心、面浮肿、四肢肿等状况。 但是长期刮痧，不加节制会造成皮外组织损伤，不但无助于缓解疲劳，还会加重身体负担，祛湿首推二 十八珍膏，精选薏苡仁、山药、葛根等二十多种祛湿食材进行古方配制与熬制，缓解身体疲劳，温和祛湿，调理肠胃健康，不会加重身体负担，有效率高达九五成以上，早就被列入非遗，网上就能找到，凡刮治部位的皮肤有溃烂、损伤、炎症都不宜用这种疗法，大病初愈、重病、气虚血亏及饱食、饥饿状态下也不宜刮痧。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	另外还要注意一下刮痧的注意事项：</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; text-align: center; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	<img _src=\"http://www.alonely.com.cn/d/file/jiankang/2017-06-28/mm1fecrghaj.jpg\" alt=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.66796875\" data-type=\"png\" src=\"http://www.alonely.com.cn/d/file/jiankang/2017-06-28/mm1fecrghaj.jpg\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	一、治疗刮痧时应避风和注意保暖</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	治疗刮痧时应避风，注意保暖。室温较低时应尽量减少暴露部位，夏季高温时不可在电扇处或有对流风处刮痧。因刮痧时皮肤汗孔开泄，如遇风寒之邪，邪气可通过开泄的毛孔直接人里，不但影响刮痧的效果，还会因感受风寒引发新的疾病。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	二、治疗刮痧后饮热水一杯<br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\" />\r\n	治疗刮痧使汁孔汗泄，邪气外排，要消耗部分体内的津液，刮痧后饮热水一杯，个但可以补充消耗部分，还能促进新陈代谢，加速代谢产物的排出。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; text-align: center; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	<img _src=\"http://7xkq88.com1.z0.glb.clouddn.com/1835669-temp-201806-03-1528011411837.jpg\" alt=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.66796875\" data-type=\"png\" src=\"http://7xkq88.com1.z0.glb.clouddn.com/1835669-temp-201806-03-1528011411837.jpg\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	三、刮痧后洗浴的时间<br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\" />\r\n	治疗刮痧后，为避免风寒之邪侵袭，须侍皮肤毛孔闭合恢复原状后，方可洗浴，一般约3小时左右。但在洗浴过程中，水渍未干时，可以刮痧。因洗浴时毛孔微微开泄，此时刮痧用时少，效果显著，但应注意保暖。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	&nbsp;</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	&nbsp;</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	&nbsp;</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	​</p>\r\n','','','182.124.21.126');
INSERT INTO `dede_addonarticle` VALUES('37','4','<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	湿气，是中医所说风、寒、暑、湿、燥、火六种病邪之一。如果体内湿气重，就会导致水湿内阻，常常引起全身的不适，其原因是湿气会侵入五脏六腑：湿在脾，则脾虚，湿在胃，则胃弱，湿在肾，则肾虚，湿在肺，则肺弱，脏六腑不调和，湿气根本不可能完全祛除。湿气会在外导致很多表症，如皮肤油腻，口干口苦，嗓子干痒，长痘，湿疹，腰酸背痛等等。那么，人为什么有湿气？湿气怎么治？</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	<img _src=\"http://p.jianke.net/article/201509/20150922111329728.png\" alt=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.66796875\" data-type=\"png\" src=\"http://p.jianke.net/article/201509/20150922111329728.png\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	人以内的湿，大都由以下两个方面造成的：第一是经络不通。第二是身体内阳气不足。经络不通，大都是因为过食垃圾食物;阳气不足，是过食冷饮啤酒。同时，猛吹空调均是造成经络不通以及阳气不足的重要原因。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	<img _src=\"http://7xkq88.com1.z0.glb.clouddn.com/1862785-temp-201806-04-1528107173596.jpg\" alt=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.66796875\" data-type=\"png\" src=\"http://7xkq88.com1.z0.glb.clouddn.com/1862785-temp-201806-04-1528107173596.jpg\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">1.饮食祛湿</strong></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	祛除体内湿气，薏米红豆粥是佳品，既能当茶喝，又能当饭吃。薏米，它可以治湿痹，利肠胃，消水肿，健脾益胃，久服轻身益气。红豆，有明显的利水、消肿、健脾胃作用，红色入心，它还有补心功用。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	在熬薏米红豆粥时，不要加大米进去。因为大米长在水里，含有湿气，湿性黏稠，所以大米一熬就稠了。红豆和薏米都是去湿的，本身不含湿，汤很清。中医恰恰是利用了清的性质，来把人体的湿除掉。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	此外，在潮湿的天气出行或者淋雨之后，适合喝上一碗热辣辣的姜汁发汗，最适合在淋雨之后驱散身体湿气，预防感冒；苦温的中药甘姜，也如同慢火，缓缓将体内水气逼散出来。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">2.运动祛湿</strong></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px;
